R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n##############################################################################\n\n# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n\n#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n#' @param x numeric vector of points\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\neval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n  vals <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  # Replace zeros with a very small number to avoid -Inf in log\n  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n\n  log(vals)\n}\n\n#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  # Compute slopes between consecutive points\n  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # For log-concavity, slopes must be non-increasing\n  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull tangent lines at each abscissa\n#' Returns a list with slope and intercept for each tangent line\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return list with vectors 'slope' and 'intercept'\ncompute_tangents <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # For interior points, use averaged slopes; for endpoints use one-sided\n  slopes <- numeric(n)\n  if (n == 1) {\n    slopes[1] <- 0\n  } else {\n    # Finite differences\n    dh <- diff(hx)\n    dx <- diff(x)\n    seg_slopes <- dh / dx\n\n    # Use segment slopes for tangent at each point\n    # At point j, the tangent is h(x_j) + h'(x_j)*(t - x_j)\n    # We approximate h'(x_j) using finite differences\n    # For the upper hull, we use the secant slopes between consecutive points\n    slopes <- seg_slopes  # length n-1, one per interval\n  }\n\n  list(seg_slopes = slopes, x = x, hx = hx)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull function u(x) at arbitrary points\n#' The upper hull is piecewise linear, defined by tangent lines at abscissae.\n#' Between x[j] and x[j+1], the upper hull is the minimum of the two tangent\n#' lines from x[j] and x[j+1]. But in the Gilks & Wild formulation, the upper\n#' hull in the interval (z[j], z[j+1]) is the tangent line at x[j].\n#'\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate upper hull\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param z intersection points of tangent lines (length n+1, including bounds)\n#' @return upper hull values at t\neval_upper_hull <- function(t, x, hx, z, slopes) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # For each t, find which segment it falls in\n  # z has n+1 entries: z[1]=lb, z[2..n]=intersections, z[n+1]=ub\n  # Segment j (1..n): z[j] <= t < z[j+1], use tangent at x[j]\n  seg <- findInterval(t, z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n))\n  hx[seg] + slopes[seg] * (t - x[seg])\n}\n\n#' Compute the lower hull function l(x) at arbitrary points\n#' The lower hull is piecewise linear between consecutive abscissae.\n#' Outside the range of abscissae, l(x) = -Inf.\n#'\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate lower hull\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return lower hull values at t\neval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n  # For points inside the abscissae range, interpolate\n  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n  if (any(inside)) {\n    ti <- t[inside]\n    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n    # Linear interpolation\n    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n  }\n  result\n}\n\n#' Compute intersection points of adjacent tangent lines\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param slopes slopes of tangent lines (h'(x_j))\n#' @param lb lower bound of domain\n#' @param ub upper bound of domain\n#' @return vector of intersection points (length n+1)\ncompute_z_points <- function(x, hx, slopes, lb, ub) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  z <- numeric(n + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[n + 1] <- ub\n  if (n >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(n - 1)) {\n      # Intersection of tangent at x[j] and x[j+1]:\n      # hx[j] + slopes[j]*(z - x[j]) = hx[j+1] + slopes[j+1]*(z - x[j+1])\n      # z = (hx[j+1] - hx[j] - slopes[j+1]*x[j+1] + slopes[j]*x[j]) / (slopes[j] - slopes[j+1])\n      denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x[j] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - slopes[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + slopes[j] * x[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  z\n}\n\n#' Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa using the derivative of h(x)\n#' We approximate using finite differences of h at nearby points\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return vector of slopes (length n)\ncompute_slopes <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n == 1) return(0)\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  sec <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # For tangent at each point, use derivative approximation\n  # Following Gilks & Wild: tangent at x_j uses slope derived from\n  # the secant between x_{j-1} and x_{j+1} for interior points\n  # For the first point, use the secant to the second\n  # For the last point, use the secant from the second-to-last\n  slopes <- numeric(n)\n  if (n == 2) {\n    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n    slopes[2] <- sec[1]\n  } else {\n    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n    slopes[n] <- sec[n - 1]\n    for (j in 2:(n - 1)) {\n      slopes[j] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j - 1]) / (x[j + 1] - x[j - 1])\n    }\n  }\n  slopes\n}\n\n#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n#' using the inverse CDF method\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param slopes tangent slopes at abscissae\n#' @param z intersection points (length n_abscissae + 1)\n#' @return vector of samples from the upper hull\nsample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, x, hx, slopes, z) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # Compute the (unnormalized) integral of exp(u(t)) over each segment\n  # In segment j: u(t) = hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n  # integral from z[j] to z[j+1] of exp(hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])) dt\n  seg_integrals <- numeric(n)\n  for (j in 1:n) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    # Shift for numerical stability: let c = hx[j] - slopes[j]*x[j]\n    # integral = exp(c) * integral of exp(sj*t) from a to b\n    cj <- hx[j] - sj * x[j]\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n    }\n    # Handle potential numerical issues\n    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n    }\n  }\n\n  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n  }\n\n  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n\n  # Sample segments\n  segments <- sample(1:n, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n\n  # Sample within each segment using inverse CDF of exponential\n  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n    j <- segments[i]\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    u <- runif(1)\n\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      # Uniform on [a, b]\n      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      # Inverse CDF: F(t) = (exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a)) / (exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))\n      # t = log(exp(sj*a) + u*(exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))) / sj\n      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n    }\n    # Clamp to segment bounds\n    samples[i] <- max(a, min(b, samples[i]))\n  }\n  samples\n}\n\n#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\ninitialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n  # Handle infinite bounds by finding a suitable finite range\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    # Try to find the mode around 0\n    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n    vals <- f(test_pts)\n    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n    # Expand outward\n    lb_eff <- center - 10\n    ub_eff <- center + 10\n  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n    ub_eff <- ub\n    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n  } else {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- ub\n  }\n\n  # Create initial abscissae spread across the effective domain\n  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n  # Remove exact endpoints if they are at the boundary\n  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n  x_init\n}\n\n#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n  }\n}\n\n# ---- Main ARS function ----\n\n#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n#'\n#' @param n number of samples to generate\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n  # Step 1: Validate inputs\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n\n  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n  }\n\n  # Step 2: Initialize abscissae\n  x_abs <- initialize_abscissae(lb, ub, f, k)\n  x_abs <- sort(unique(x_abs))\n\n  # Evaluate log-density at initial abscissae\n  hx <- eval_log_density(x_abs, f)\n\n  # Step 3: Check initial log-concavity\n  check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n\n  # Step 4: Main sampling loop\n  samples <- numeric(0)\n  max_iter <- n * 100  # Safety limit to prevent infinite loops\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (length(samples) < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa\n    slopes_vec <- compute_slopes(x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Compute intersection points z\n    z <- compute_z_points(x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, lb, ub)\n\n    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, z)\n\n    # Evaluate upper and lower hulls at x_star\n    u_star <- eval_upper_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx, z, slopes_vec)\n    l_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    if (w <= exp(l_star - u_star)) {\n      # Accept by squeezing test\n      samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n    } else {\n      # Evaluate the actual log-density\n      h_star <- eval_log_density(x_star, f)\n\n      # Rejection test\n      if (w <= exp(h_star - u_star)) {\n        samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n      }\n\n      # Update the abscissae: add x_star\n      insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n      hx <- append(hx, h_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n\n      # Re-check log-concavity with new point\n      check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (length(samples) < n) {\n    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n  }\n\n  samples[1:min(n, length(samples))]\n}\n\n# ---- Test function ----\n\n#' Run formal tests of the ARS implementation\n#' Tests compare ARS samples against known distributions using\n#' Kolmogorov-Smirnov tests and moment comparisons.\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  # Helper to report test results\n  report <- function(name, passed, details = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: PASS\\n\", name))\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: FAIL\\n\", name))\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(details) > 0) cat(sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", details))\n  }\n\n  # ---- Test 1: Input validation ----\n  cat(\"--- Input Validation Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test negative n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(-5, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Negative_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test non-integer n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(3.5, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Non_integer_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test non-function f\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(100, \"not_a_function\")\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Non_function_f_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test lb >= ub\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(100, dnorm, lb = 5, ub = 2)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Invalid_bounds_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test zero n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(0, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Zero_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Log-Concavity Check Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: non-log-concave density (bimodal mixture)\n  bimodal <- function(x) {\n    0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = -3, sd = 0.5) + 0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = 3, sd = 0.5)\n  }\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(1000, bimodal, lb = -10, ub = 10)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    grepl(\"[Nn]on-log-concav\", e$message)\n  })\n  report(\"Bimodal_non_log_concave_detected\", passed)\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Standard Normal Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: standard normal\n  set.seed(42)\n  samps <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps)) {\n    m <- mean(samps)\n    s <- sd(samps)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~0)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", s))\n\n    # KS test against standard normal\n    ks <- ks.test(samps, \"pnorm\", mean = 0, sd = 1)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Normal_mean_close_to_zero\", abs(m) < 0.15,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", m))\n    report(\"Normal_sd_close_to_one\", abs(s - 1) < 0.15,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", s))\n    report(\"Normal_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n\n    # Save samples\n    writeLines(as.character(samps), \"/app/normal_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved samples to /app/normal_samples.txt\\n\")\n  } else {\n    report(\"Normal_mean_close_to_zero\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal_sd_close_to_one\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Exponential Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: exponential distribution (rate=2)\n  set.seed(123)\n  exp_density <- function(x) dexp(x, rate = 2)\n  samps_exp <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = exp_density, lb = 0, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_exp)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_exp)\n    s <- sd(samps_exp)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~0.5)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~0.5)\\n\", s))\n\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_exp, \"pexp\", rate = 2)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Exponential_mean_correct\", abs(m - 0.5) < 0.1,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=0.5, tolerance=0.1\", m))\n    report(\"Exponential_sd_correct\", abs(s - 0.5) < 0.1,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=0.5, tolerance=0.1\", s))\n    report(\"Exponential_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n\n    writeLines(as.character(samps_exp), \"/app/exponential_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved samples to /app/exponential_samples.txt\\n\")\n  } else {\n    report(\"Exponential_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Exponential_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Exponential_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Gamma Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: Gamma(shape=3, rate=1) -- log-concave for shape >= 1\n  set.seed(456)\n  gamma_density <- function(x) dgamma(x, shape = 3, rate = 1)\n  samps_gam <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = gamma_density, lb = 0, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_gam)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_gam)\n    s <- sd(samps_gam)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~3)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~1.73)\\n\", s))\n\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_gam, \"pgamma\", shape = 3, rate = 1)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Gamma_mean_correct\", abs(m - 3) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=3.0, tolerance=0.3\", m))\n    report(\"Gamma_sd_correct\", abs(s - sqrt(3)) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=1.73, tolerance=0.3\", s))\n    report(\"Gamma_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Gamma_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Gamma_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Gamma_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Beta Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: Beta(2,5) -- log-concave for alpha >= 1, beta >= 1\n  set.seed(789)\n  beta_density <- function(x) dbeta(x, shape1 = 2, shape2 = 5)\n  samps_beta <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = beta_density, lb = 0, ub = 1), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_beta)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_beta)\n    s <- sd(samps_beta)\n    expected_mean <- 2 / 7\n    expected_sd <- sqrt(2 * 5 / (49 * 8))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\", m, expected_mean))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\", s, expected_sd))\n\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_beta, \"pbeta\", shape1 = 2, shape2 = 5)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Beta_mean_correct\", abs(m - expected_mean) < 0.05,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=%.4f, tolerance=0.05\", m, expected_mean))\n    report(\"Beta_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Beta_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Beta_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Normal with Shifted Mean Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: Normal(mean=5, sd=2)\n  set.seed(101)\n  norm5_density <- function(x) dnorm(x, mean = 5, sd = 2)\n  samps_n5 <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = norm5_density, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_n5)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_n5)\n    s <- sd(samps_n5)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~5)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~2)\\n\", s))\n\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_n5, \"pnorm\", mean = 5, sd = 2)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Normal5_mean_correct\", abs(m - 5) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=5.0, tolerance=0.3\", m))\n    report(\"Normal5_sd_correct\", abs(s - 2) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=2.0, tolerance=0.3\", s))\n    report(\"Normal5_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Normal5_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal5_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal5_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Module/Helper Function Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: eval_log_density\n  ld <- eval_log_density(c(0, 1), dnorm)\n  expected_ld <- log(dnorm(c(0, 1)))\n  passed <- all(abs(ld - expected_ld) < 1e-10)\n  report(\"eval_log_density_correct\", passed,\n         sprintf(\"got [%.6f, %.6f], expected [%.6f, %.6f]\",\n                 ld[1], ld[2], expected_ld[1], expected_ld[2]))\n\n  # {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01EJoVVTWZ6e9hx1zAmUaXzs","type":"tool_result","content":"File created successfully at: /app/ars.R"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3423f84b-e35a-4cfe-80f8-e811e643317f","uuid":"a38b393d-5d51-425c-9200-991b837b8727","tool_use_result":{"type":"create","filePath":"/app/ars.R","content":"##############################################################################\n# Adaptive Rejection Sampling (ARS)\n# Based on Gilks, W. R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n##############################################################################\n\n# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n\n#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n#' @param x numeric vector of points\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\neval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n  vals <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  # Replace zeros with a very small number to avoid -Inf in log\n  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n\n  log(vals)\n}\n\n#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  # Compute slopes between consecutive points\n  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # For log-concavity, slopes must be non-increasing\n  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull tangent lines at each abscissa\n#' Returns a list with slope and intercept for each tangent line\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return list with vectors 'slope' and 'intercept'\ncompute_tangents <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # For interior points, use averaged slopes; for endpoints use one-sided\n  slopes <- numeric(n)\n  if (n == 1) {\n    slopes[1] <- 0\n  } else {\n    # Finite differences\n    dh <- diff(hx)\n    dx <- diff(x)\n    seg_slopes <- dh / dx\n\n    # Use segment slopes for tangent at each point\n    # At point j, the tangent is h(x_j) + h'(x_j)*(t - x_j)\n    # We approximate h'(x_j) using finite differences\n    # For the upper hull, we use the secant slopes between consecutive points\n    slopes <- seg_slopes  # length n-1, one per interval\n  }\n\n  list(seg_slopes = slopes, x = x, hx = hx)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull function u(x) at arbitrary points\n#' The upper hull is piecewise linear, defined by tangent lines at abscissae.\n#' Between x[j] and x[j+1], the upper hull is the minimum of the two tangent\n#' lines from x[j] and x[j+1]. But in the Gilks & Wild formulation, the upper\n#' hull in the interval (z[j], z[j+1]) is the tangent line at x[j].\n#'\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate upper hull\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param z intersection points of tangent lines (length n+1, including bounds)\n#' @return upper hull values at t\neval_upper_hull <- function(t, x, hx, z, slopes) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # For each t, find which segment it falls in\n  # z has n+1 entries: z[1]=lb, z[2..n]=intersections, z[n+1]=ub\n  # Segment j (1..n): z[j] <= t < z[j+1], use tangent at x[j]\n  seg <- findInterval(t, z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n))\n  hx[seg] + slopes[seg] * (t - x[seg])\n}\n\n#' Compute the lower hull function l(x) at arbitrary points\n#' The lower hull is piecewise linear between consecutive abscissae.\n#' Outside the range of abscissae, l(x) = -Inf.\n#'\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate lower hull\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return lower hull values at t\neval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n  # For points inside the abscissae range, interpolate\n  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n  if (any(inside)) {\n    ti <- t[inside]\n    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n    # Linear interpolation\n    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n  }\n  result\n}\n\n#' Compute intersection points of adjacent tangent lines\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param slopes slopes of tangent lines (h'(x_j))\n#' @param lb lower bound of domain\n#' @param ub upper bound of domain\n#' @return vector of intersection points (length n+1)\ncompute_z_points <- function(x, hx, slopes, lb, ub) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  z <- numeric(n + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[n + 1] <- ub\n  if (n >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(n - 1)) {\n      # Intersection of tangent at x[j] and x[j+1]:\n      # hx[j] + slopes[j]*(z - x[j]) = hx[j+1] + slopes[j+1]*(z - x[j+1])\n      # z = (hx[j+1] - hx[j] - slopes[j+1]*x[j+1] + slopes[j]*x[j]) / (slopes[j] - slopes[j+1])\n      denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x[j] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - slopes[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + slopes[j] * x[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  z\n}\n\n#' Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa using the derivative of h(x)\n#' We approximate using finite differences of h at nearby points\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return vector of slopes (length n)\ncompute_slopes <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n == 1) return(0)\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  sec <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # For tangent at each point, use derivative approximation\n  # Following Gilks & Wild: tangent at x_j uses slope derived from\n  # the secant between x_{j-1} and x_{j+1} for interior points\n  # For the first point, use the secant to the second\n  # For the last point, use the secant from the second-to-last\n  slopes <- numeric(n)\n  if (n == 2) {\n    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n    slopes[2] <- sec[1]\n  } else {\n    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n    slopes[n] <- sec[n - 1]\n    for (j in 2:(n - 1)) {\n      slopes[j] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j - 1]) / (x[j + 1] - x[j - 1])\n    }\n  }\n  slopes\n}\n\n#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n#' using the inverse CDF method\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param slopes tangent slopes at abscissae\n#' @param z intersection points (length n_abscissae + 1)\n#' @return vector of samples from the upper hull\nsample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, x, hx, slopes, z) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # Compute the (unnormalized) integral of exp(u(t)) over each segment\n  # In segment j: u(t) = hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n  # integral from z[j] to z[j+1] of exp(hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])) dt\n  seg_integrals <- numeric(n)\n  for (j in 1:n) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    # Shift for numerical stability: let c = hx[j] - slopes[j]*x[j]\n    # integral = exp(c) * integral of exp(sj*t) from a to b\n    cj <- hx[j] - sj * x[j]\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n    }\n    # Handle potential numerical issues\n    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n    }\n  }\n\n  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n  }\n\n  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n\n  # Sample segments\n  segments <- sample(1:n, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n\n  # Sample within each segment using inverse CDF of exponential\n  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n    j <- segments[i]\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    u <- runif(1)\n\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      # Uniform on [a, b]\n      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      # Inverse CDF: F(t) = (exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a)) / (exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))\n      # t = log(exp(sj*a) + u*(exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))) / sj\n      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n    }\n    # Clamp to segment bounds\n    samples[i] <- max(a, min(b, samples[i]))\n  }\n  samples\n}\n\n#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\ninitialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n  # Handle infinite bounds by finding a suitable finite range\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    # Try to find the mode around 0\n    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n    vals <- f(test_pts)\n    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n    # Expand outward\n    lb_eff <- center - 10\n    ub_eff <- center + 10\n  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n    ub_eff <- ub\n    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n  } else {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- ub\n  }\n\n  # Create initial abscissae spread across the effective domain\n  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n  # Remove exact endpoints if they are at the boundary\n  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n  x_init\n}\n\n#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n  }\n}\n\n# ---- Main ARS function ----\n\n#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n#'\n#' @param n number of samples to generate\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n  # Step 1: Validate inputs\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n\n  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n  }\n\n  # Step 2: Initialize abscissae\n  x_abs <- initialize_abscissae(lb, ub, f, k)\n  x_abs <- sort(unique(x_abs))\n\n  # Evaluate log-density at initial abscissae\n  hx <- eval_log_density(x_abs, f)\n\n  # Step 3: Check initial log-concavity\n  check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n\n  # Step 4: Main sampling loop\n  samples <- numeric(0)\n  max_iter <- n * 100  # Safety limit to prevent infinite loops\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (length(samples) < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa\n    slopes_vec <- compute_slopes(x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Compute intersection points z\n    z <- compute_z_points(x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, lb, ub)\n\n    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, z)\n\n    # Evaluate upper and lower hulls at x_star\n    u_star <- eval_upper_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx, z, slopes_vec)\n    l_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    if (w <= exp(l_star - u_star)) {\n      # Accept by squeezing test\n      samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n    } else {\n      # Evaluate the actual log-density\n      h_star <- eval_log_density(x_star, f)\n\n      # Rejection test\n      if (w <= exp(h_star - u_star)) {\n        samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n      }\n\n      # Update the abscissae: add x_star\n      insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n      hx <- append(hx, h_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n\n      # Re-check log-concavity with new point\n      check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (length(samples) < n) {\n    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n  }\n\n  samples[1:min(n, length(samples))]\n}\n\n# ---- Test function ----\n\n#' Run formal tests of the ARS implementation\n#' Tests compare ARS samples against known distributions using\n#' Kolmogorov-Smirnov tests and moment comparisons.\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  # Helper to report test results\n  report <- function(name, passed, details = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: PASS\\n\", name))\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: FAIL\\n\", name))\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(details) > 0) cat(sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", details))\n  }\n\n  # ---- Test 1: Input validation ----\n  cat(\"--- Input Validation Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test negative n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(-5, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Negative_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test non-integer n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(3.5, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Non_integer_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test non-function f\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(100, \"not_a_function\")\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Non_function_f_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test lb >= ub\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(100, dnorm, lb = 5, ub = 2)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Invalid_bounds_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test zero n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(0, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Zero_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Log-Concavity Check Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: non-log-concave density (bimodal mixture)\n  bimodal <- function(x) {\n    0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = -3, sd = 0.5) + 0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = 3, sd = 0.5)\n  }\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(1000, bimodal, lb = -10, ub = 10)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    grepl(\"[Nn]on-log-concav\", e$message)\n  })\n  report(\"Bimodal_non_log_concave_detected\", passed)\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Standard Normal Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: standard normal\n  set.seed(42)\n  samps <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps)) {\n    m <- mean(samps)\n    s <- sd(samps)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~0)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", s))\n\n    # KS test against standard normal\n    ks <- ks.test(samps, \"pnorm\", mean = 0, sd = 1)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Normal_mean_close_to_zero\", abs(m) < 0.15,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", m))\n    report(\"Normal_sd_close_to_one\", abs(s - 1) < 0.15,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", s))\n    report(\"Normal_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n\n    # R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n     4→# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n     5→##############################################################################\n     6→\n     7→# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n     8→\n     9→#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n    10→#' @param x numeric vector of points\n    11→#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n    12→#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\n    13→eval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n    14→  vals <- f(x)\n    15→  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    16→    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n    17→  }\n    18→  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    19→    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n    20→  }\n    21→  # Replace zeros with a very small number to avoid -Inf in log\n    22→  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n    23→\n    24→  log(vals)\n    25→}\n    26→\n    27→#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n    28→#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n    29→#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n    30→#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\n    31→check_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n    32→  n <- length(x)\n    33→  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n    34→  # Compute slopes between consecutive points\n    35→  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n    36→  # For log-concavity, slopes must be non-increasing\n    37→  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n    38→  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    39→    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n    40→  }\n    41→  return(TRUE)\n    42→}\n    43→\n    44→#' Compute the upper hull tangent lines at each abscissa\n    45→#' Returns a list with slope and intercept for each tangent line\n    46→#' @param x sorted abscissae\n    47→#' @param hx log-density at x\n    48→#' @return list with vectors 'slope' and 'intercept'\n    49→compute_tangents <- function(x, hx) {\n    50→  n <- length(x)\n    51→  # For interior points, use averaged slopes; for endpoints use one-sided\n    52→  slopes <- numeric(n)\n    53→  if (n == 1) {\n    54→    slopes[1] <- 0\n    55→  } else {\n    56→    # Finite differences\n    57→    dh <- diff(hx)\n    58→    dx <- diff(x)\n    59→    seg_slopes <- dh / dx\n    60→\n    61→    # Use segment slopes for tangent at each point\n    62→    # At point j, the tangent is h(x_j) + h'(x_j)*(t - x_j)\n    63→    # We approximate h'(x_j) using finite differences\n    64→    # For the upper hull, we use the secant slopes between consecutive points\n    65→    slopes <- seg_slopes  # length n-1, one per interval\n    66→  }\n    67→\n    68→  list(seg_slopes = slopes, x = x, hx = hx)\n    69→}\n    70→\n    71→#' Compute the upper hull function u(x) at arbitrary points\n    72→#' The upper hull is piecewise linear, defined by tangent lines at abscissae.\n    73→#' Between x[j] and x[j+1], the upper hull is the minimum of the two tangent\n    74→#' lines from x[j] and x[j+1]. But in the Gilks & Wild formulation, the upper\n    75→#' hull in the interval (z[j], z[j+1]) is the tangent line at x[j].\n    76→#'\n    77→#' @param t points at which to evaluate upper hull\n    78→#' @param x sorted abscissae\n    79→#' @param hx log-density at x\n    80→#' @param z intersection points of tangent lines (length n+1, including bounds)\n    81→#' @return upper hull values at t\n    82→eval_upper_hull <- function(t, x, hx, z, slopes) {\n    83→  n <- length(x)\n    84→  # For each t, find which segment it falls in\n    85→  # z has n+1 entries: z[1]=lb, z[2..n]=intersections, z[n+1]=ub\n    86→  # Segment j (1..n): z[j] <= t < z[j+1], use tangent at x[j]\n    87→  seg <- findInterval(t, z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    88→  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n))\n    89→  hx[seg] + slopes[seg] * (t - x[seg])\n    90→}\n    91→\n    92→#' Compute the lower hull function l(x) at arbitrary points\n    93→#' The lower hull is piecewise linear between consecutive abscissae.\n    94→#' Outside the range of abscissae, l(x) = -Inf.\n    95→#'\n    96→#' @param t points at which to evaluate lower hull\n    97→#' @param x sorted abscissae\n    98→#' @param hx log-density at x\n    99→#' @return lower hull values at t\n   100→eval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n   101→  n <- length(x)\n   102→  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n   103→  # For points inside the abscissae range, interpolate\n   104→  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n   105→  if (any(inside)) {\n   106→    ti <- t[inside]\n   107→    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n   108→    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n   109→    # Linear interpolation\n   110→    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n   111→    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n   112→  }\n   113→  result\n   114→}\n   115→\n   116→#' Compute intersection points of adjacent tangent lines\n   117→#' @param x sorted abscissae\n   118→#' @param hx log-density at x\n   119→#' @param slopes slopes of tangent lines (h'(x_j))\n   120→#' @param lb lower bound of domain\n   121→#' @param ub upper bound of domain\n   122→#' @return vector of intersection points (length n+1)\n   123→compute_z_points <- function(x, hx, slopes, lb, ub) {\n   124→  n <- length(x)\n   125→  z <- numeric(n + 1)\n   126→  z[1] <- lb\n   127→  z[n + 1] <- ub\n   128→  if (n >= 2) {\n   129→    for (j in 1:(n - 1)) {\n   130→      # Intersection of tangent at x[j] and x[j+1]:\n   131→      # hx[j] + slopes[j]*(z - x[j]) = hx[j+1] + slopes[j+1]*(z - x[j+1])\n   132→      # z = (hx[j+1] - hx[j] - slopes[j+1]*x[j+1] + slopes[j]*x[j]) / (slopes[j] - slopes[j+1])\n   133→      denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n   134→      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n   135→        z[j + 1] <- (x[j] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n   136→      } else {\n   137→        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - slopes[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + slopes[j] * x[j]) / denom\n   138→      }\n   139→    }\n   140→  }\n   141→  z\n   142→}\n   143→\n   144→#' Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa using the derivative of h(x)\n   145→#' We approximate using finite differences of h at nearby points\n   146→#' @param x sorted abscissae\n   147→#' @param hx log-density at x\n   148→#' @return vector of slopes (length n)\n   149→compute_slopes <- function(x, hx) {\n   150→  n <- length(x)\n   151→  if (n == 1) return(0)\n   152→  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n   153→  sec <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n   154→  # For tangent at each point, use derivative approximation\n   155→  # Following Gilks & Wild: tangent at x_j uses slope derived from\n   156→  # the secant between x_{j-1} and x_{j+1} for interior points\n   157→  # For the first point, use the secant to the second\n   158→  # For the last point, use the secant from the second-to-last\n   159→  slopes <- numeric(n)\n   160→  if (n == 2) {\n   161→    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n   162→    slopes[2] <- sec[1]\n   163→  } else {\n   164→    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n   165→    slopes[n] <- sec[n - 1]\n   166→    for (j in 2:(n - 1)) {\n   167→      slopes[j] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j - 1]) / (x[j + 1] - x[j - 1])\n   168→    }\n   169→  }\n   170→  slopes\n   171→}\n   172→\n   173→#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n   174→#' using the inverse CDF method\n   175→#' @param n number of samples\n   176→#' @param x sorted abscissae\n   177→#' @param hx log-density at x\n   178→#' @param slopes tangent slopes at abscissae\n   179→#' @param z intersection points (length n_abscissae + 1)\n   180→#' @return vector of samples from the upper hull\n   181→sample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, x, hx, slopes, z) {\n   182→  n <- length(x)\n   183→  # Compute the (unnormalized) integral of exp(u(t)) over each segment\n   184→  # In segment j: u(t) = hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n   185→  # integral from z[j] to z[j+1] of exp(hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])) dt\n   186→  seg_integrals <- numeric(n)\n   187→  for (j in 1:n) {\n   188→    a <- z[j]\n   189→    b <- z[j + 1]\n   190→    sj <- slopes[j]\n   191→    # Shift for numerical stability: let c = hx[j] - slopes[j]*x[j]\n   192→    # integral = exp(c) * integral of exp(sj*t) from a to b\n   193→    cj <- hx[j] - sj * x[j]\n   194→    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n   195→      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (b - a)\n   196→    } else {\n   197→      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n   198→    }\n   199→    # Handle potential numerical issues\n   200→    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n   201→      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n   202→    }\n   203→  }\n   204→\n   205→  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n   206→  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n   207→    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n   208→  }\n   209→\n   210→  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n   211→\n   212→  # Sample segments\n   213→  segments <- sample(1:n, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n   214→\n   215→  # Sample within each segment using inverse CDF of exponential\n   216→  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n   217→  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n   218→    j <- segments[i]\n   219→    a <- z[j]\n   220→    b <- z[j + 1]\n   221→    sj <- slopes[j]\n   222→    u <- runif(1)\n   223→\n   224→    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n   225→      # Uniform on [a, b]\n   226→      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n   227→    } else {\n   228→      # Inverse CDF: F(t) = (exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a)) / (exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))\n   229→      # t = log(exp(sj*a) + u*(exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))) / sj\n   230→      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n   231→      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n   232→      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n   233→      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n   234→      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n   235→    }\n   236→    # Clamp to segment bounds\n   237→    samples[i] <- max(a, min(b, samples[i]))\n   238→  }\n   239→  samples\n   240→}\n   241→\n   242→#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n   243→#' @param lb lower bound\n   244→#' @param ub upper bound\n   245→#' @param f density function\n   246→#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n   247→#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\n   248→initialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n   249→  # Handle infinite bounds by finding a suitable finite range\n   250→  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n   251→    # Try to find the mode around 0\n   252→    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n   253→    vals <- f(test_pts)\n   254→    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n   255→    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n   256→    # Expand outward\n   257→    lb_eff <- center - 10\n   258→    ub_eff <- center + 10\n   259→  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n   260→    ub_eff <- ub\n   261→    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n   262→  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n   263→    lb_eff <- lb\n   264→    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n   265→  } else {\n   266→    lb_eff <- lb\n   267→    ub_eff <- ub\n   268→  }\n   269→\n   270→  # Create initial abscissae spread across the effective domain\n   271→  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n   272→  # Remove exact endpoints if they are at the boundary\n   273→  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n   274→  x_init\n   275→}\n   276→\n   277→#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n   278→#' @param n number of samples\n   279→#' @param f density function\n   280→#' @param lb lower bound\n   281→#' @param ub upper bound\n   282→validate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n   283→  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n   284→    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n   285→  }\n   286→  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n   287→    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n   288→  }\n   289→  if (!is.function(f)) {\n   290→    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n   291→  }\n   292→  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n   293→    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n   294→  }\n   295→  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n   296→    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n   297→  }\n   298→  if (lb >= ub) {\n   299→    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n   300→  }\n   301→}\n   302→\n   303→# ---- Main ARS function ----\n   304→\n   305→#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n   306→#'\n   307→#' @param n number of samples to generate\n   308→#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n   309→#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n   310→#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n   311→#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n   312→#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\n   313→ars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n   314→  # Step 1: Validate inputs\n   315→  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n   316→\n   317→  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n   318→    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n   319→  }\n   320→\n   321→  # Step 2: Initialize abscissae\n   322→  x_abs <- initialize_abscissae(lb, ub, f, k)\n   323→  x_abs <- sort(unique(x_abs))\n   324→\n   325→  # Evaluate log-density at initial abscissae\n   326→  hx <- eval_log_density(x_abs, f)\n   327→\n   328→  # Step 3: Check initial log-concavity\n   329→  check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n   330→\n   331→  # Step 4: Main sampling loop\n   332→  samples <- numeric(0)\n   333→  max_iter <- n * 100  # Safety limit to prevent infinite loops\n   334→  iter <- 0\n   335→\n   336→  while (length(samples) < n && iter < max_iter) {\n   337→    iter <- iter + 1\n   338→\n   339→    # Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa\n   340→    slopes_vec <- compute_slopes(x_abs, hx)\n   341→\n   342→    # Compute intersection points z\n   343→    z <- compute_z_points(x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, lb, ub)\n   344→\n   345→    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n   346→    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, z)\n   347→\n   348→    # Evaluate upper and lower hulls at x_star\n   349→    u_star <- eval_upper_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx, z, slopes_vec)\n   350→    l_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx)\n   351→\n   352→    # Squeeze test\n   353→    w <- runif(1)\n   354→    if (w <= exp(l_star - u_star)) {\n   355→      # Accept by squeezing test\n   356→      samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n   357→    } else {\n   358→      # Evaluate the actual log-density\n   359→      h_star <- eval_log_density(x_star, f)\n   360→\n   361→      # Rejection test\n   362→      if (w <= exp(h_star - u_star)) {\n   363→        samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n   364→      }\n   365→\n   366→      # Update the abscissae: add x_star\n   367→      insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n   368→      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n   369→      hx <- append(hx, h_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n   370→\n   371→      # Re-check log-concavity with new point\n   372→      check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n   373→    }\n   374→  }\n   375→\n   376→  if (length(samples) < n) {\n   377→    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n   378→  }\n   379→\n   380→  samples[1:min(n, length(samples))]\n   381→}\n   382→\n   383→# ---- Test function ----\n   384→\n   385→#' Run formal tests of the ARS implementation\n   386→#' Tests compare ARS samples against known distributions using\n   387→#' Kolmogorov-Smirnov tests and moment comparisons.\n   388→test <- function() {\n   389→  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n   390→  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n   391→  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n   392→\n   393→  pass_count <- 0\n   394→  fail_count <- 0\n   395→\n   396→  # Helper to report test results\n   397→  report <- function(name, passed, details = \"\") {\n   398→    if (passed) {\n   399→      cat(sprintf(\"%s: PASS\\n\", name))\n   400→      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n   401→    } else {\n   402→      cat(sprintf(\"%s: FAIL\\n\", name))\n   403→      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n   404→    }\n   405→    if (nchar(details) > 0) cat(sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", details))\n   406→  }\n   407→\n   408→  # ---- Test 1: Input validation ----\n   409→  cat(\"--- Input Validation Tests ---\\n\")\n   410→\n   411→  # Test negative n\n   412→  passed <- tryCatch({\n   413→    ars(-5, dnorm)\n   414→    FALSE\n   415→  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n   416→  report(\"Negative_n_rejected\", passed)\n   417→\n   418→  # Test non-integer n\n   419→  passed <- tryCatch({\n   420→    ars(3.5, dnorm)\n   421→    FALSE\n   422→  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n   423→  report(\"Non_integer_n_rejected\", passed)\n   424→\n   425→  # Test non-function f\n   426→  passed <- tryCatch({\n   427→    ars(100, \"not_a_function\")\n   428→    FALSE\n   429→  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n   430→  report(\"Non_function_f_rejected\", passed)\n   431→\n   432→  # Test lb >= ub\n   433→  passed <- tryCatch({\n   434→    ars(100, dnorm, lb = 5, ub = 2)\n   435→    FALSE\n   436→  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n   437→  report(\"Invalid_bounds_rejected\", passed)\n   438→\n   439→  # Test zero n\n   440→  passed <- tryCatch({\n   441→    ars(0, dnorm)\n   442→    FALSE\n   443→  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n   444→  report(\"Zero_n_rejected\", passed)\n   445→\n   446→  cat(\"\\n--- Log-Concavity Check Tests ---\\n\")\n   447→\n   448→  # Test: non-log-concave density (bimodal mixture)\n   449→  bimodal <- function(x) {\n   450→    0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = -3, sd = 0.5) + 0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = 3, sd = 0.5)\n   451→  }\n   452→  passed <- tryCatch({\n   453→    ars(1000, bimodal, lb = -10, ub = 10)\n   454→    FALSE\n   455→  }, error = function(e) {\n   456→    grepl(\"[Nn]on-log-concav\", e$message)\n   457→  })\n   458→  report(\"Bimodal_non_log_concave_detected\", passed)\n   459→\n   460→  cat(\"\\n--- Standard Normal Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n   461→\n   462→  # Test: standard normal\n   463→  set.seed(42)\n   464→  samps <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n   465→    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n   466→    NULL\n   467→  })\n   468→\n   469→  if (!is.null(samps)) {\n   470→    m <- mean(samps)\n   471→    s <- sd(samps)\n   472→    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~0)\\n\", m))\n   473→    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", s))\n   474→\n   475→    # KS test against standard normal\n   476→    ks <- ks.test(samps, \"pnorm\", mean = 0, sd = 1)\n   477→    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n   478→\n   479→    report(\"Normal_mean_close_to_zero\", abs(m) < 0.15,\n   480→           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", m))\n   481→    report(\"Normal_sd_close_to_one\", abs(s - 1) < 0.15,\n   482→           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", s))\n   483→    report(\"Normal_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n   484→           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n   485→\n   486→    # Test: Beta(2,5) -- log-concave for alpha >= 1, beta >= 1\n   563→  set.seed(789)\n   564→  beta_density <- function(x) dbeta(x, shape1 = 2, shape2 = 5)\n   565→  samps_beta <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = beta_density, lb = 0, ub = 1), error = function(e) {\n   566→    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n   567→    NULL\n   568→  })\n   569→\n   570→  if (!is.null(samps_beta)) {\n   571→    m <- mean(samps_beta)\n   572→    s <- sd(samps_beta)\n   573→    expected_mean <- 2 / 7\n   574→    expected_sd <- sqrt(2 * 5 / (49 * 8))\n   575→    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\", m, expected_mean))\n   576→    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\", s, expected_sd))\n   577→\n   578→    ks <- ks.test(samps_beta, \"pbeta\", shape1 = 2, shape2 = 5)\n   579→    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n   580→\n   581→    report(\"Beta_mean_correct\", abs(m - expected_mean) < 0.05,\n   582→           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=%.4f, tolerance=0.05\", m, expected_mean))\n   583→    report(\"Beta_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n   584→           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n   585→  } else {\n   586→    report(\"Beta_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n   587→    report(\"Beta_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n   588→  }\n   589→\n   590→  cat(\"\\n--- Normal with Shifted Mean Tests ---\\n\")\n   591→\n   592→  # R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n##############################################################################\n\n# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n\n#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n#' @param x numeric vector of points\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\neval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n  vals <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  # Replace zeros with a very small number to avoid -Inf in log\n  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n\n  log(vals)\n}\n\n#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  # Compute slopes between consecutive points\n  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # For log-concavity, slopes must be non-increasing\n  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull tangent lines at each abscissa\n#' Returns a list with slope and intercept for each tangent line\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return list with vectors 'slope' and 'intercept'\ncompute_tangents <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # For interior points, use averaged slopes; for endpoints use one-sided\n  slopes <- numeric(n)\n  if (n == 1) {\n    slopes[1] <- 0\n  } else {\n    # Finite differences\n    dh <- diff(hx)\n    dx <- diff(x)\n    seg_slopes <- dh / dx\n\n    # Use segment slopes for tangent at each point\n    # At point j, the tangent is h(x_j) + h'(x_j)*(t - x_j)\n    # We approximate h'(x_j) using finite differences\n    # For the upper hull, we use the secant slopes between consecutive points\n    slopes <- seg_slopes  # length n-1, one per interval\n  }\n\n  list(seg_slopes = slopes, x = x, hx = hx)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull function u(x) at arbitrary points\n#' The upper hull is piecewise linear, defined by tangent lines at abscissae.\n#' Between x[j] and x[j+1], the upper hull is the minimum of the two tangent\n#' lines from x[j] and x[j+1]. But in the Gilks & Wild formulation, the upper\n#' hull in the interval (z[j], z[j+1]) is the tangent line at x[j].\n#'\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate upper hull\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param z intersection points of tangent lines (length n+1, including bounds)\n#' @return upper hull values at t\neval_upper_hull <- function(t, x, hx, z, slopes) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # For each t, find which segment it falls in\n  # z has n+1 entries: z[1]=lb, z[2..n]=intersections, z[n+1]=ub\n  # Segment j (1..n): z[j] <= t < z[j+1], use tangent at x[j]\n  seg <- findInterval(t, z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n))\n  hx[seg] + slopes[seg] * (t - x[seg])\n}\n\n#' Compute the lower hull function l(x) at arbitrary points\n#' The lower hull is piecewise linear between consecutive abscissae.\n#' Outside the range of abscissae, l(x) = -Inf.\n#'\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate lower hull\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return lower hull values at t\neval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n  # For points inside the abscissae range, interpolate\n  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n  if (any(inside)) {\n    ti <- t[inside]\n    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n    # Linear interpolation\n    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n  }\n  result\n}\n\n#' Compute intersection points of adjacent tangent lines\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param slopes slopes of tangent lines (h'(x_j))\n#' @param lb lower bound of domain\n#' @param ub upper bound of domain\n#' @return vector of intersection points (length n+1)\ncompute_z_points <- function(x, hx, slopes, lb, ub) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  z <- numeric(n + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[n + 1] <- ub\n  if (n >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(n - 1)) {\n      # Intersection of tangent at x[j] and x[j+1]:\n      # hx[j] + slopes[j]*(z - x[j]) = hx[j+1] + slopes[j+1]*(z - x[j+1])\n      # z = (hx[j+1] - hx[j] - slopes[j+1]*x[j+1] + slopes[j]*x[j]) / (slopes[j] - slopes[j+1])\n      denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x[j] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - slopes[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + slopes[j] * x[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  z\n}\n\n#' Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa using the derivative of h(x)\n#' We approximate using finite differences of h at nearby points\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return vector of slopes (length n)\ncompute_slopes <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n == 1) return(0)\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  sec <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # For tangent at each point, use derivative approximation\n  # Following Gilks & Wild: tangent at x_j uses slope derived from\n  # the secant between x_{j-1} and x_{j+1} for interior points\n  # For the first point, use the secant to the second\n  # For the last point, use the secant from the second-to-last\n  slopes <- numeric(n)\n  if (n == 2) {\n    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n    slopes[2] <- sec[1]\n  } else {\n    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n    slopes[n] <- sec[n - 1]\n    for (j in 2:(n - 1)) {\n      slopes[j] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j - 1]) / (x[j + 1] - x[j - 1])\n    }\n  }\n  slopes\n}\n\n#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n#' using the inverse CDF method\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param slopes tangent slopes at abscissae\n#' @param z intersection points (length n_abscissae + 1)\n#' @return vector of samples from the upper hull\nsample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, x, hx, slopes, z) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # Compute the (unnormalized) integral of exp(u(t)) over each segment\n  # In segment j: u(t) = hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n  # integral from z[j] to z[j+1] of exp(hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])) dt\n  seg_integrals <- numeric(n)\n  for (j in 1:n) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    # Shift for numerical stability: let c = hx[j] - slopes[j]*x[j]\n    # integral = exp(c) * integral of exp(sj*t) from a to b\n    cj <- hx[j] - sj * x[j]\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n    }\n    # Handle potential numerical issues\n    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n    }\n  }\n\n  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n  }\n\n  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n\n  # Sample segments\n  segments <- sample(1:n, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n\n  # Sample within each segment using inverse CDF of exponential\n  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n    j <- segments[i]\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    u <- runif(1)\n\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      # Uniform on [a, b]\n      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      # Inverse CDF: F(t) = (exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a)) / (exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))\n      # t = log(exp(sj*a) + u*(exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))) / sj\n      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n    }\n    # Clamp to segment bounds\n    samples[i] <- max(a, min(b, samples[i]))\n  }\n  samples\n}\n\n#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\ninitialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n  # Handle infinite bounds by finding a suitable finite range\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    # Try to find the mode around 0\n    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n    vals <- f(test_pts)\n    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n    # Expand outward\n    lb_eff <- center - 10\n    ub_eff <- center + 10\n  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n    ub_eff <- ub\n    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n  } else {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- ub\n  }\n\n  # Create initial abscissae spread across the effective domain\n  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n  # Remove exact endpoints if they are at the boundary\n  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n  x_init\n}\n\n#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n  }\n}\n\n# ---- Main ARS function ----\n\n#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n#'\n#' @param n number of samples to generate\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n  # Step 1: Validate inputs\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n\n  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n  }\n\n  # Step 2: Initialize abscissae\n  x_abs <- initialize_abscissae(lb, ub, f, k)\n  x_abs <- sort(unique(x_abs))\n\n  # Evaluate log-density at initial abscissae\n  hx <- eval_log_density(x_abs, f)\n\n  # Step 3: Check initial log-concavity\n  check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n\n  # Step 4: Main sampling loop\n  samples <- numeric(0)\n  max_iter <- n * 100  # Safety limit to prevent infinite loops\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (length(samples) < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa\n    slopes_vec <- compute_slopes(x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Compute intersection points z\n    z <- compute_z_points(x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, lb, ub)\n\n    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, z)\n\n    # Evaluate upper and lower hulls at x_star\n    u_star <- eval_upper_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx, z, slopes_vec)\n    l_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    if (w <= exp(l_star - u_star)) {\n      # Accept by squeezing test\n      samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n    } else {\n      # Evaluate the actual log-density\n      h_star <- eval_log_density(x_star, f)\n\n      # Rejection test\n      if (w <= exp(h_star - u_star)) {\n        samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n      }\n\n      # Update the abscissae: add x_star\n      insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n      hx <- append(hx, h_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n\n      # Re-check log-concavity with new point\n      check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (length(samples) < n) {\n    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n  }\n\n  samples[1:min(n, length(samples))]\n}\n\n# ---- Test function ----\n\n#' Run formal tests of the ARS implementation\n#' Tests compare ARS samples against known distributions using\n#' Kolmogorov-Smirnov tests and moment comparisons.\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  # Helper to report test results\n  report <- function(name, passed, details = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: PASS\\n\", name))\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: FAIL\\n\", name))\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(details) > 0) cat(sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", details))\n  }\n\n  # ---- Test 1: Input validation ----\n  cat(\"--- Input Validation Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test negative n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(-5, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Negative_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test non-integer n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(3.5, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Non_integer_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test non-function f\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(100, \"not_a_function\")\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Non_function_f_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test lb >= ub\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(100, dnorm, lb = 5, ub = 2)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Invalid_bounds_rejected\", passed)\n\n  # Test zero n\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(0, dnorm)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Zero_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Log-Concavity Check Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: non-log-concave density (bimodal mixture)\n  bimodal <- function(x) {\n    0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = -3, sd = 0.5) + 0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = 3, sd = 0.5)\n  }\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(1000, bimodal, lb = -10, ub = 10)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    grepl(\"[Nn]on-log-concav\", e$message)\n  })\n  report(\"Bimodal_non_log_concave_detected\", passed)\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Standard Normal Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: standard normal\n  set.seed(42)\n  samps <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps)) {\n    m <- mean(samps)\n    s <- sd(samps)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~0)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", s))\n\n    # KS test against standard normal\n    ks <- ks.test(samps, \"pnorm\", mean = 0, sd = 1)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Normal_mean_close_to_zero\", abs(m) < 0.15,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", m))\n    report(\"Normal_sd_close_to_one\", abs(s - 1) < 0.15,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", s))\n    report(\"Normal_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n\n    # Save samples\n    writeLines(as.character(samps), \"/app/normal_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved samples to /app/normal_samples.txt\\n\")\n  } else {\n    report(\"Normal_mean_close_to_zero\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal_sd_close_to_one\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Exponential Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: exponential distribution (rate=2)\n  set.seed(123)\n  exp_density <- function(x) dexp(x, rate = 2)\n  samps_exp <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = exp_density, lb = 0, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_exp)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_exp)\n    s <- sd(samps_exp)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~0.5)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~0.5)\\n\", s))\n\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_exp, \"pexp\", rate = 2)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Exponential_mean_correct\", abs(m - 0.5) < 0.1,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=0.5, tolerance=0.1\", m))\n    report(\"Exponential_sd_correct\", abs(s - 0.5) < 0.1,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=0.5, tolerance=0.1\", s))\n    report(\"Exponential_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n\n    writeLines(as.character(samps_exp), \"/app/exponential_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved samples to /app/exponential_samples.txt\\n\")\n  } else {\n    report(\"Exponential_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Exponential_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Exponential_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Gamma Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: Gamma(shape=3, rate=1) -- log-concave for shape >= 1\n  set.seed(456)\n  gamma_density <- function(x) dgamma(x, shape = 3, rate = 1)\n  samps_gam <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = gamma_density, lb = 0, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_gam)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_gam)\n    s <- sd(samps_gam)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~3)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~1.73)\\n\", s))\n\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_gam, \"pgamma\", shape = 3, rate = 1)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Gamma_mean_correct\", abs(m - 3) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=3.0, tolerance=0.3\", m))\n    report(\"Gamma_sd_correct\", abs(s - sqrt(3)) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=1.73, tolerance=0.3\", s))\n    report(\"Gamma_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Gamma_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Gamma_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Gamma_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Beta Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: Beta(2,5) -- log-concave for alpha >= 1, beta >= 1\n  set.seed(789)\n  beta_density <- function(x) dbeta(x, shape1 = 2, shape2 = 5)\n  samps_beta <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = beta_density, lb = 0, ub = 1), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_beta)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_beta)\n    s <- sd(samps_beta)\n    expected_mean <- 2 / 7\n    expected_sd <- sqrt(2 * 5 / (49 * 8))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\", m, expected_mean))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\", s, expected_sd))\n\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_beta, \"pbeta\", shape1 = 2, shape2 = 5)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Beta_mean_correct\", abs(m - expected_mean) < 0.05,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=%.4f, tolerance=0.05\", m, expected_mean))\n    report(\"Beta_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Beta_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Beta_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Normal with Shifted Mean Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: Normal(mean=5, sd=2)\n  set.seed(101)\n  norm5_density <- function(x) dnorm(x, mean = 5, sd = 2)\n  samps_n5 <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = norm5_density, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_n5)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_n5)\n    s <- sd(samps_n5)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~5)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~2)\\n\", s))\n\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_n5, \"pnorm\", mean = 5, sd = 2)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n\n    report(\"Normal5_mean_correct\", abs(m - 5) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=5.0, tolerance=0.3\", m))\n    report(\"Normal5_sd_correct\", abs(s - 2) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=2.0, tolerance=0.3\", s))\n    report(\"Normal5_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Normal5_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal5_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal5_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Module/Helper Function Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # Test: eval_log_density\n  ld <- eval_log_density(c(0, 1), dnorm)\n  expected_ld <- log(dnorm(c(0, 1)))\n  passed <- all(abs(ld - expected_ld) < 1e-10)\n  report(\"eval_log_density_correct\", passed,\n         sprintf(\"got [%.6f, %.6f], expected [%.6f, %.6f]\",\n                 ld[1], ld[2], expected_ld[1], expected_ld[2]))\n\n  #
