{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_01YHPG9pHvBdk91ZCTYEBYyR","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01N1n2gjfVu22aXEyCH59Hix","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/app/ars.R","content":"##############################################################################\n# Adaptive Rejection Sampling (ARS)\n# Based on Gilks, W. R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n##############################################################################\n\n# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n\n#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n#' @param x numeric vector of points\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\neval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n  vals <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n  log(vals)\n}\n\n#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull using secant-based construction\n#' For a log-concave h, the secant between (x_j, h_j) and (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1})\n#' lies ABOVE h(x) for x outside [x_j, x_{j+1}].\n#'\n#' Upper hull construction:\n#' - Piece 1 (left of x_1 to some z_1): line through x_1 & x_2\n#' - Piece j (z_{j-1} to z_j) for interior: line through x_{j-1} & x_j\n#' - Piece k (right of z_{k-1}): line through x_{k-1} & x_k\n#'\n#' z_j = intersection of line through (x_j, x_{j+1}) with line through (x_{j+1}, x_{j+2})\n#'\n#' @param x sorted abscissae (length >= 2)\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @return list with slopes, intercepts, z (breakpoints), n_pieces\nbuild_upper_hull <- function(x, hx, lb, ub) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive abscissae\n  sec_slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # Number of line pieces = n-1 (one per consecutive pair)\n  n_pieces <- n - 1\n\n  # Each piece j uses the line through (x_j, h_j) and (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1})\n  # which has slope sec_slopes[j] and passes through (x_j, h_j)\n  # u_j(t) = h_j + sec_slopes[j] * (t - x_j)\n\n  # Breakpoints z: length n_pieces + 1\n  # z[1] = lb, z[n_pieces+1] = ub\n  # z[j+1] = intersection of piece j and piece j+1\n  z <- numeric(n_pieces + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[n_pieces + 1] <- ub\n\n  if (n_pieces >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(n_pieces - 1)) {\n      # Piece j: hx[j] + sec_slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n      # Piece j+1: hx[j+1] + sec_slopes[j+1]*(t - x[j+1])\n      # Intersection:\n      # hx[j] + sec_slopes[j]*(t - x[j]) = hx[j+1] + sec_slopes[j+1]*(t - x[j+1])\n      # t*(sec_slopes[j] - sec_slopes[j+1]) = hx[j+1] - hx[j] - sec_slopes[j+1]*x[j+1] + sec_slopes[j]*x[j]\n      denom <- sec_slopes[j] - sec_slopes[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x[j + 1] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - sec_slopes[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + sec_slopes[j] * x[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Ensure z is sorted (numerical safety)\n  for (i in 2:length(z)) {\n    if (!is.na(z[i]) && !is.na(z[i-1]) && is.finite(z[i]) && is.finite(z[i-1])) {\n      if (z[i] < z[i-1]) z[i] <- z[i-1]\n    }\n  }\n\n  list(\n    slopes = sec_slopes,\n    x = x,\n    hx = hx,\n    z = z,\n    n_pieces = n_pieces\n  )\n}\n\n#' Evaluate the upper hull at arbitrary points\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate\n#' @param hull upper hull object from build_upper_hull\n#' @return upper hull values at t\neval_upper_hull <- function(t, hull) {\n  seg <- findInterval(t, hull$z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, hull$n_pieces))\n  # Piece j uses line through (x[j], hx[j]) with slope slopes[j]\n  hull$hx[seg] + hull$slopes[seg] * (t - hull$x[seg])\n}\n\n#' Evaluate the lower hull at arbitrary points\n#' The lower hull is piecewise linear connecting consecutive abscissae.\n#' Outside the range of abscissae, l(x) = -Inf.\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return lower hull values at t\neval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n  if (any(inside)) {\n    ti <- t[inside]\n    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n  }\n  result\n}\n\n#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n#' @param nsamp number of samples\n#' @param hull upper hull object from build_upper_hull\n#' @return vector of samples\nsample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, hull) {\n  np <- hull$n_pieces\n  z <- hull$z\n  slopes <- hull$slopes\n  x <- hull$x\n  hx <- hull$hx\n\n  # Compute integral of exp(u(t)) over each piece\n  # Piece j: u(t) = hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n  # Let cj = hx[j] - slopes[j]*x[j], then u(t) = cj + slopes[j]*t\n  # Integral = exp(cj) * integral of exp(slopes[j]*t) dt from z[j] to z[j+1]\n  seg_integrals <- numeric(np)\n  cj_vec <- hx[1:np] - slopes * x[1:np]\n\n  for (j in 1:np) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n\n    # Handle infinite bounds for integration\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      if (sj <= 0) {\n        # exp(cj + sj*t) from -Inf: integral diverges if sj <= 0\n        # This shouldn't happen for a proper upper hull\n        seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n        next\n      }\n      # exp(cj) * (exp(sj*b) - 0) / sj = exp(cj + sj*b) / sj\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj_vec[j] + sj * b) / sj\n      next\n    }\n    if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      if (sj >= 0) {\n        seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n        next\n      }\n      # exp(cj) * (0 - exp(sj*a)) / sj = -exp(cj + sj*a) / sj\n      seg_integrals[j] <- -exp(cj_vec[j] + sj * a) / sj\n      next\n    }\n\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj_vec[j]) * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj_vec[j]) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n    }\n    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n    }\n  }\n\n  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n  }\n\n  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n  segments <- sample(1:np, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n\n  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n    j <- segments[i]\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    u <- runif(1)\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      # sj > 0 guaranteed (otherwise integral = 0)\n      # CDF: F(t) = exp(sj*t) / exp(sj*b) for t in (-Inf, b]\n      # Inverse: t = b + log(u) / sj\n      samples[i] <- b + log(u) / sj\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      # sj < 0 guaranteed\n      # CDF: F(t) = 1 - exp(sj*(t - a)) / ... hmm\n      # integral from a to t of exp(cj + sj*s) ds = exp(cj)*(exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a))/sj\n      # total = -exp(cj + sj*a)/sj\n      # CDF = (exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a)) / (0 - exp(sj*a)) = 1 - exp(sj*(t-a))\n      # u = 1 - exp(sj*(t-a))\n      # t = a + log(1 - u) / sj\n      samples[i] <- a + log(1 - u) / sj\n    } else if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n    }\n    # Clamp to segment bounds (finite only)\n    if (is.finite(a)) samples[i] <- max(a, samples[i])\n    if (is.finite(b)) samples[i] <- min(b, samples[i])\n  }\n  samples\n}\n\n#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\ninitialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n    vals <- f(test_pts)\n    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n    lb_eff <- center - 10\n    ub_eff <- center + 10\n  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n    ub_eff <- ub\n    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n  } else {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- ub\n  }\n\n  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n  x_init\n}\n\n#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n  }\n}\n\n# ---- Main ARS function ----\n\n#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n#'\n#' @param n number of samples to generate\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n  # Step 1: Validate inputs\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n\n  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n  }\n\n  # Step 2: Initialize abscissae\n  x_abs <- initialize_abscissae(lb, ub, f, k)\n  x_abs <- sort(unique(x_abs))\n\n  # Evaluate log-density at initial abscissae\n  hx <- eval_log_density(x_abs, f)\n\n  # Step 3: Check initial log-concavity\n  check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n\n  # Step 4: Main sampling loop\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  n_accepted <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (n_accepted < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Build upper hull from current abscissae\n    hull <- build_upper_hull(x_abs, hx, lb, ub)\n\n    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, hull)\n\n    # Evaluate upper and lower hulls at x_star\n    u_star <- eval_upper_hull(x_star, hull)\n    l_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    if (w <= exp(l_star - u_star)) {\n      n_accepted <- n_accepted + 1\n      samples[n_accepted] <- x_star\n    } else {\n      # Evaluate the actual log-density\n      h_star <- eval_log_density(x_star, f)\n\n      # Rejection test\n      if (w <= exp(h_star - u_star)) {\n        n_accepted <- n_accepted + 1\n        samples[n_accepted] <- x_star\n      }\n\n      # Update the abscissae: add x_star (cap at 200 to prevent slowdown)\n      if (length(x_abs) < 200) {\n        insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n        x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n        hx <- append(hx, h_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n\n        # Re-check log-concavity with new point\n        check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (n_accepted < n) {\n    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n    return(samples[1:n_accepted])\n  }\n\n  samples\n}\n\n# ---- Test function ----\n\n#' Run formal tests of the ARS implementation\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  report <- function(name, passed, details = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: PASS\\n\", name))\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: FAIL\\n\", name))\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(details) > 0) cat(sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", details))\n  }\n\n  # ---- Input Validation Tests ----\n  cat(\"--- Input Validation Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  passed <- tryCatch({ ars(-5, dnorm); FALSE }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Negative_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  passed <- tryCatch({ ars(3.5, report(\"Non_function_f_rejected\", passed)\n\n  passed <- tryCatch({ ars(100, dnorm, lb = 5, ub = 2); FALSE }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Invalid_bounds_rejected\", passed)\n\n  passed <- R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n##############################################################################\n\n# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n\n#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n#' @param x numeric vector of points\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\neval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n  vals <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n  log(vals)\n}\n\n#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull using secant-based construction\n#' For a log-concave h, the secant between (x_j, h_j) and (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1})\n#' lies ABOVE h(x) for x outside [x_j, x_{j+1}].\n#'\n#' Upper hull construction:\n#' - Piece 1 (left of x_1 to some z_1): line through x_1 & x_2\n#' - Piece j (z_{j-1} to z_j) for interior: line through x_{j-1} & x_j\n#' - Piece k (right of z_{k-1}): line through x_{k-1} & x_k\n#'\n#' z_j = intersection of line through (x_j, x_{j+1}) with line through (x_{j+1}, x_{j+2})\n#'\n#' @param x sorted abscissae (length >= 2)\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @return list with slopes, intercepts, z (breakpoints), n_pieces\nbuild_upper_hull <- function(x, hx, lb, ub) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive abscissae\n  sec_slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # Number of line pieces = n-1 (one per consecutive pair)\n  n_pieces <- n - 1\n\n  # Each piece j uses the line through (x_j, h_j) and (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1})\n  # which has slope sec_slopes[j] and passes through (x_j, h_j)\n  # u_j(t) = h_j + sec_slopes[j] * (t - x_j)\n\n  # Breakpoints z: length n_pieces + 1\n  # z[1] = lb, z[n_pieces+1] = ub\n  # z[j+1] = intersection of piece j and piece j+1\n  z <- numeric(n_pieces + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[n_pieces + 1] <- ub\n\n  if (n_pieces >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(n_pieces - 1)) {\n      # Piece j: hx[j] + sec_slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n      # Piece j+1: hx[j+1] + sec_slopes[j+1]*(t - x[j+1])\n      # Intersection:\n      # hx[j] + sec_slopes[j]*(t - x[j]) = hx[j+1] + sec_slopes[j+1]*(t - x[j+1])\n      # t*(sec_slopes[j] - sec_slopes[j+1]) = hx[j+1] - hx[j] - sec_slopes[j+1]*x[j+1] + sec_slopes[j]*x[j]\n      denom <- sec_slopes[j] - sec_slopes[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x[j + 1] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - sec_slopes[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + sec_slopes[j] * x[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Ensure z is sorted (numerical safety)\n  for (i in 2:length(z)) {\n    if (!is.na(z[i]) && !is.na(z[i-1]) && is.finite(z[i]) && is.finite(z[i-1])) {\n      if (z[i] < z[i-1]) z[i] <- z[i-1]\n    }\n  }\n\n  list(\n    slopes = sec_slopes,\n    x = x,\n    hx = hx,\n    z = z,\n    n_pieces = n_pieces\n  )\n}\n\n#' Evaluate the upper hull at arbitrary points\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate\n#' @param hull upper hull object from build_upper_hull\n#' @return upper hull values at t\neval_upper_hull <- function(t, hull) {\n  seg <- findInterval(t, hull$z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, hull$n_pieces))\n  # Piece j uses line through (x[j], hx[j]) with slope slopes[j]\n  hull$hx[seg] + hull$slopes[seg] * (t - hull$x[seg])\n}\n\n#' Evaluate the lower hull at arbitrary points\n#' The lower hull is piecewise linear connecting consecutive abscissae.\n#' Outside the range of abscissae, l(x) = -Inf.\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return lower hull values at t\neval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n  if (any(inside)) {\n    ti <- t[inside]\n    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n  }\n  result\n}\n\n#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n#' @param nsamp number of samples\n#' @param hull upper hull object from build_upper_hull\n#' @return vector of samples\nsample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, hull) {\n  np <- hull$n_pieces\n  z <- hull$z\n  slopes <- hull$slopes\n  x <- hull$x\n  hx <- hull$hx\n\n  # Compute integral of exp(u(t)) over each piece\n  # Piece j: u(t) = hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n  # Let cj = hx[j] - slopes[j]*x[j], then u(t) = cj + slopes[j]*t\n  # Integral = exp(cj) * integral of exp(slopes[j]*t) dt from z[j] to z[j+1]\n  seg_integrals <- numeric(np)\n  cj_vec <- hx[1:np] - slopes * x[1:np]\n\n  for (j in 1:np) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n\n    # Handle infinite bounds for integration\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      if (sj <= 0) {\n        # exp(cj + sj*t) from -Inf: integral diverges if sj <= 0\n        # This shouldn't happen for a proper upper hull\n        seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n        next\n      }\n      # exp(cj) * (exp(sj*b) - 0) / sj = exp(cj + sj*b) / sj\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj_vec[j] + sj * b) / sj\n      next\n    }\n    if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      if (sj >= 0) {\n        seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n        next\n      }\n      # exp(cj) * (0 - exp(sj*a)) / sj = -exp(cj + sj*a) / sj\n      seg_integrals[j] <- -exp(cj_vec[j] + sj * a) / sj\n      next\n    }\n\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj_vec[j]) * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj_vec[j]) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n    }\n    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n    }\n  }\n\n  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n  }\n\n  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n  segments <- sample(1:np, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n\n  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n    j <- segments[i]\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    u <- runif(1)\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      # sj > 0 guaranteed (otherwise integral = 0)\n      # CDF: F(t) = exp(sj*t) / exp(sj*b) for t in (-Inf, b]\n      # Inverse: t = b + log(u) / sj\n      samples[i] <- b + log(u) / sj\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      # sj < 0 guaranteed\n      # CDF: F(t) = 1 - exp(sj*(t - a)) / ... hmm\n      # integral from a to t of exp(cj + sj*s) ds = exp(cj)*(exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a))/sj\n      # total = -exp(cj + sj*a)/sj\n      # CDF = (exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a)) / (0 - exp(sj*a)) = 1 - exp(sj*(t-a))\n      # u = 1 - exp(sj*(t-a))\n      # t = a + log(1 - u) / sj\n      samples[i] <- a + log(1 - u) / sj\n    } else if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n    }\n    # Clamp to segment bounds (finite only)\n    if (is.finite(a)) samples[i] <- max(a, samples[i])\n    if (is.finite(b)) samples[i] <- min(b, samples[i])\n  }\n  samples\n}\n\n#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\ninitialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n    vals <- f(test_pts)\n    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n    lb_eff <- center - 10\n    ub_eff <- center + 10\n  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n    ub_eff <- ub\n    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n  } else {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- ub\n  }\n\n  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n  x_init\n}\n\n#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n  }\n}\n\n# ---- Main ARS function ----\n\n#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n#'\n#' @param n number of samples to generate\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n  # Step 1: Validate inputs\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n\n  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n  }\n\n  # Step 2: Initialize abscissae\n  x_abs <- initialize_abscissae(lb, ub, f, k)\n  x_abs <- sort(unique(x_abs))\n\n  # Evaluate log-density at initial abscissae\n  hx <- eval_log_density(x_abs, f)\n\n  # Step 3: Check initial log-concavity\n  check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n\n  # Step 4: Main sampling loop\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  n_accepted <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (n_accepted < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Build upper hull from current abscissae\n    hull <- build_upper_hull(x_abs, hx, lb, ub)\n\n    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, hull)\n\n    # Evaluate upper and lower hulls at x_star\n    u_star <- eval_upper_hull(x_star, hull)\n    l_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    if (w <= exp(l_star - u_star)) {\n      n_accepted <- n_accepted + 1\n      samples[n_accepted] <- x_star\n    } else {\n      # Evaluate the actual log-density\n      h_star <- eval_log_density(x_star, f)\n\n      # Rejection test\n      if (w <= exp(h_star - u_star)) {\n        n_accepted <- n_accepted + 1\n        samples[n_accepted] <- x_star\n      }\n\n      # Update the abscissae: add x_star (cap at 200 to prevent slowdown)\n      if (length(x_abs) < 200) {\n        insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n        x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n        hx <- append(hx, h_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n\n        # Re-check log-concavity with new point\n        check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (n_accepted < n) {\n    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n    return(samples[1:n_accepted])\n  }\n\n  samples\n}\n\n# ---- Test function ----\n\n#' Run formal tests of the ARS implementation\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  report <- function(name, passed, details = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: PASS\\n\", name))\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(sprintf(\"%s: FAIL\\n\", name))\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(details) > 0) cat(sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", details))\n  }\n\n  # ---- Input Validation Tests ----\n  cat(\"--- Input Validation Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  passed <- tryCatch({ ars(-5, dnorm); FALSE }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Negative_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  passed <- tryCatch({ ars(3.5, dnorm); FALSE }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Non_integer_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  passed <- tryCatch({ ars(100, \"not_a_function\"); FALSE }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Non_function_f_rejected\", passed)\n\n  passed <- tryCatch({ ars(100, dnorm, lb = 5, ub = 2); FALSE }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Invalid_bounds_rejected\", passed)\n\n  passed <- tryCatch({ ars(0, dnorm); FALSE }, error = function(e) TRUE)\n  report(\"Zero_n_rejected\", passed)\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Log-Concavity Check Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  bimodal <- function(x) {\n    0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = -3, sd = 0.5) + 0.5 * dnorm(x, mean = 3, sd = 0.5)\n  }\n  passed <- tryCatch({\n    ars(1000, bimodal, lb = -10, ub = 10)\n    FALSE\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    grepl(\"[Nn]on-log-concav\", e$message)\n  })\n  report(\"Bimodal_non_log_concave_detected\", passed)\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Standard Normal Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  set.seed(42)\n  samps <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps)) {\n    m <- mean(samps)\n    s <- sd(samps)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~0)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samps, \"pnorm\", mean = 0, sd = 1)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    report(\"Normal_mean_close_to_zero\", abs(m) < 0.15,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", m))\n    report(\"Normal_sd_close_to_one\", abs(s - 1) < 0.15,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, tolerance=0.15\", s))\n    report(\"Normal_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n    writeLines(as.character(samps), \"/app/normal_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved samples to /app/normal_samples.txt\\n\")\n  } else {\n    report(\"Normal_mean_close_to_zero\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal_sd_close_to_one\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Exponential Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  set.seed(123)\n  exp_density <- function(x) dexp(x, rate = 2)\n  samps_exp <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = exp_density, lb = 0, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_exp)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_exp)\n    s <- sd(samps_exp)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~0.5)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~0.5)\\n\", s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_exp, \"pexp\", rate = 2)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    report(\"Exponential_mean_correct\", abs(m - 0.5) < 0.1,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=0.5, tolerance=0.1\", m))\n    report(\"Exponential_sd_correct\", abs(s - 0.5) < 0.1,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=0.5, tolerance=0.1\", s))\n    report(\"Exponential_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n    writeLines(as.character(samps_exp), \"/app/exponential_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved samples to /app/exponential_samples.txt\\n\")\n  } else {\n    report(\"Exponential_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Exponential_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Exponential_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Gamma Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  set.seed(456)\n  gamma_density <- function(x) dgamma(x, shape = 3, rate = 1)\n  samps_gam <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = gamma_density, lb = 0, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_gam)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_gam)\n    s <- sd(samps_gam)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~3)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~1.73)\\n\", s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_gam, \"pgamma\", shape = 3, rate = 1)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    report(\"Gamma_mean_correct\", abs(m - 3) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=3.0, tolerance=0.3\", m))\n    report(\"Gamma_sd_correct\", abs(s - sqrt(3)) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=1.73, tolerance=0.3\", s))\n    report(\"Gamma_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Gamma_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Gamma_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Gamma_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Beta Distribution Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  set.seed(789)\n  beta_density <- function(x) dbeta(x, shape1 = 2, shape2 = 5)\n  samps_beta <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = beta_density, lb = 0, ub = 1), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_beta)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_beta)\n    s <- sd(samps_beta)\n    expected_mean <- 2 / 7\n    expected_sd <- sqrt(2 * 5 / (49 * 8))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\", m, expected_mean))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\", s, expected_sd))\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_beta, \"pbeta\", shape1 = 2, shape2 = 5)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    report(\"Beta_mean_correct\", abs(m - expected_mean) < 0.05,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=%.4f, tolerance=0.05\", m, expected_mean))\n    report(\"Beta_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Beta_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Beta_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Normal with Shifted Mean Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  set.seed(101)\n  norm5_density <- function(x) dnorm(x, mean = 5, sd = 2)\n  samps_n5 <- tryCatch(ars(n = 2000, f = norm5_density, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf), error = function(e) {\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Error: %s\\n\", e$message))\n    NULL\n  })\n\n  if (!is.null(samps_n5)) {\n    m <- mean(samps_n5)\n    s <- sd(samps_n5)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean: %.4f (expected ~5)\\n\", m))\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample sd:   %.4f (expected ~2)\\n\", s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samps_n5, \"pnorm\", mean = 5, sd = 2)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value: %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    report(\"Normal5_mean_correct\", abs(m - 5) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, expected=5.0, tolerance=0.3\", m))\n    report(\"Normal5_sd_correct\", abs(s - 2) < 0.3,\n           sprintf(\"sd=%.4f, expected=2.0, tolerance=0.3\", s))\n    report(\"Normal5_KS_test_pass\", ks$p.value > 0.01,\n           sprintf(\"p=%.4f, threshold=0.01\", ks$p.value))\n  } else {\n    report(\"Normal5_mean_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal5_sd_correct\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n    report(\"Normal5_KS_test_pass\", FALSE, \"Sampling failed\")\n  }\n\n  cat(\"\\n--- Module/Helper Function Tests ---\\n\")\n\n  # eval_log_density correctness\n  ld <- eval_log_density(c(0, 1), dnorm)\n  expected_ld <- log(dnorm(c(0, 1)))\n  passed <- all(abs(ld - expected_ld) < 1e-10)\n  report(\"eval_log_density_correct\", passed,\n         sprintf(\"got [%.6f, %.6f], expected [%.6f, %.6f]\",\n                 ld[1], ld[2], expected_ld[1], expected_ld[2]))\n\n  # log-concavity check with concave data\n  x_test <- c(-2, 0, 2)\n  hx_test <- log(dnorm(x_test))\n  passed <- tryCatch({ Only auto-run if --run-tests flag is passed","-}"]}],"originalFile":"##############################################################################\n# Adaptive Rejection Sampling (ARS)\n# Based on Gilks, W. R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n##############################################################################\n\n# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n\n#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n#' @param x numeric vector of points\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\neval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n  vals <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  # Replace zeros with a very small number to avoid -Inf in log\n  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n\n  log(vals)\n}\n\n#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  # Compute slopes between consecutive points\n  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # For log-concavity, slopes must be non-increasing\n  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull tangent lines at each abscissa\n#' Returns a list with slope and intercept for each tangent line\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return list with vectors 'slope' and 'intercept'\ncompute_tangents <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # For interior points, use averaged slopes; for endpoints use one-sided\n  slopes <- numeric(n)\n  if (n == 1) {\n    slopes[1] <- 0\n  } else {\n    # Finite differences\n    dh <- diff(hx)\n    dx <- diff(x)\n    seg_slopes <- dh / dx\n\n    # Use segment slopes for tangent at each point\n    # At point j, the tangent is h(x_j) + h'(x_j)*(t - x_j)\n    # We approximate h'(x_j) using finite differences\n    # For the upper hull, we use the secant slopes between consecutive points\n    slopes <- seg_slopes  # length n-1, one per interval\n  }\n\n  list(seg_slopes = slopes, x = x, hx = hx)\n}\n\n#' Compute the upper hull function u(x) at arbitrary points\n#' The upper hull is piecewise linear, defined by tangent lines at abscissae.\n#' Between x[j] and x[j+1], the upper hull is the minimum of the two tangent\n#' lines from x[j] and x[j+1]. But in the Gilks & Wild formulation, the upper\n#' hull in the interval (z[j], z[j+1]) is the tangent line at x[j].\n#'\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate upper hull\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param z intersection points of tangent lines (length n+1, including bounds)\n#' @return upper hull values at t\neval_upper_hull <- function(t, x, hx, z, slopes) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # For each t, find which segment it falls in\n  # z has n+1 entries: z[1]=lb, z[2..n]=intersections, z[n+1]=ub\n  # Segment j (1..n): z[j] <= t < z[j+1], use tangent at x[j]\n  seg <- findInterval(t, z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n))\n  hx[seg] + slopes[seg] * (t - x[seg])\n}\n\n#' Compute the lower hull function l(x) at arbitrary points\n#' The lower hull is piecewise linear between consecutive abscissae.\n#' Outside the range of abscissae, l(x) = -Inf.\n#'\n#' @param t points at which to evaluate lower hull\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return lower hull values at t\neval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n  # For points inside the abscissae range, interpolate\n  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n  if (any(inside)) {\n    ti <- t[inside]\n    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n    # Linear interpolation\n    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n  }\n  result\n}\n\n#' Compute intersection points of adjacent tangent lines\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param slopes slopes of tangent lines (h'(x_j))\n#' @param lb lower bound of domain\n#' @param ub upper bound of domain\n#' @return vector of intersection points (length n+1)\ncompute_z_points <- function(x, hx, slopes, lb, ub) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  z <- numeric(n + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[n + 1] <- ub\n  if (n >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(n - 1)) {\n      # Intersection of tangent at x[j] and x[j+1]:\n      # hx[j] + slopes[j]*(z - x[j]) = hx[j+1] + slopes[j+1]*(z - x[j+1])\n      # z = (hx[j+1] - hx[j] - slopes[j+1]*x[j+1] + slopes[j]*x[j]) / (slopes[j] - slopes[j+1])\n      denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x[j] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - slopes[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + slopes[j] * x[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  z\n}\n\n#' Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa using the derivative of h(x)\n#' We approximate using finite differences of h at nearby points\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return vector of slopes (length n)\ncompute_slopes <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n == 1) return(0)\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  sec <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  # For tangent at each point, use derivative approximation\n  # Following Gilks & Wild: tangent at x_j uses slope derived from\n  # the secant between x_{j-1} and x_{j+1} for interior points\n  # For the first point, use the secant to the second\n  # For the last point, use the secant from the second-to-last\n  slopes <- numeric(n)\n  if (n == 2) {\n    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n    slopes[2] <- sec[1]\n  } else {\n    slopes[1] <- sec[1]\n    slopes[n] <- sec[n - 1]\n    for (j in 2:(n - 1)) {\n      slopes[j] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j - 1]) / (x[j + 1] - x[j - 1])\n    }\n  }\n  slopes\n}\n\n#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n#' using the inverse CDF method\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param slopes tangent slopes at abscissae\n#' @param z intersection points (length n_abscissae + 1)\n#' @return vector of samples from the upper hull\nsample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, x, hx, slopes, z) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  # Compute the (unnormalized) integral of exp(u(t)) over each segment\n  # In segment j: u(t) = hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])\n  # integral from z[j] to z[j+1] of exp(hx[j] + slopes[j]*(t - x[j])) dt\n  seg_integrals <- numeric(n)\n  for (j in 1:n) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    # Shift for numerical stability: let c = hx[j] - slopes[j]*x[j]\n    # integral = exp(c) * integral of exp(sj*t) from a to b\n    cj <- hx[j] - sj * x[j]\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n    }\n    # Handle potential numerical issues\n    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n    }\n  }\n\n  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n  }\n\n  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n\n  # Sample segments\n  segments <- sample(1:n, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n\n  # Sample within each segment using inverse CDF of exponential\n  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n    j <- segments[i]\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- slopes[j]\n    u <- runif(1)\n\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      # Uniform on [a, b]\n      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      # Inverse CDF: F(t) = (exp(sj*t) - exp(sj*a)) / (exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))\n      # t = log(exp(sj*a) + u*(exp(sj*b) - exp(sj*a))) / sj\n      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n    }\n    # Clamp to segment bounds\n    samples[i] <- max(a, min(b, samples[i]))\n  }\n  samples\n}\n\n#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\ninitialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n  # Handle infinite bounds by finding a suitable finite range\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    # Try to find the mode around 0\n    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n    vals <- f(test_pts)\n    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n    # Expand outward\n    lb_eff <- center - 10\n    ub_eff <- center + 10\n  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n    ub_eff <- ub\n    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n  } else {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- ub\n  }\n\n  # Create initial abscissae spread across the effective domain\n  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n  # Remove exact endpoints if they are at the boundary\n  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n  x_init\n}\n\n#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n  }\n}\n\n# ---- Main ARS function ----\n\n#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n#'\n#' @param n number of samples to generate\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n  # Step 1: Validate inputs\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n\n  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n  }\n\n  # Step 2: Initialize abscissae\n  x_abs <- initialize_abscissae(lb, ub, f, k)\n  x_abs <- sort(unique(x_abs))\n\n  # Evaluate log-density at initial abscissae\n  hx <- eval_log_density(x_abs, f)\n\n  # Step 3: Check initial log-concavity\n  check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n\n  # Step 4: Main sampling loop\n  samples <- numeric(0)\n  max_iter <- n * 100  # Safety limit to prevent infinite loops\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (length(samples) < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Compute tangent slopes at each abscissa\n    slopes_vec <- compute_slopes(x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Compute intersection points z\n    z <- compute_z_points(x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, lb, ub)\n\n    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, x_abs, hx, slopes_vec, z)\n\n    # Evaluate upper and lower hulls at x_star\n    u_star <- eval_upper_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx, z, slopes_vec)\n    l_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    if (w <= exp(l_star - u_star)) {\n      # Accept by squeezing test\n      samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n    } else {\n      # Evaluate the actual log-density\n      h_star <- eval_log_density(x_star, f)\n\n      # Rejection test\n      if (w <= exp(h_star - u_star)) {\n        samples <- c(samples, x_star)\n      }\n\n      # Update the abscissae: add x_star\n      insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n      hx <- append(hx, h_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n\n      # Re-check log-concavity with new point\n      check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (length(samples) < n) {\n    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n  }\n\n  samples[1:min(n, length(samples))]\n}\n\n# ---- Test function ----\n\n#' Run formal tests of the ARS implementation\n#' Tests compare ARS samples against known distributions using\n#' Kolmogorov-Smirnov tests and moment comparisons.\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  # Upper hull is NOT above log-density (this is a fundamental issue)\n\nThe problem is with my secant-based upper hull construction. For a log-concave function, secants between consecutive points lie BELOW h(x) between those points and ABOVE outside. But my upper hull pieces use these secants, which means between the two points defining a secant, the \"upper hull\" is actually BELOW h(x). This is wrong!\n \nI need to reconsider how the upper hull is actually constructed in Gilks & Wild. The secants don't directly form the hull pieces—instead, the hull uses outer secants that properly bound the function from above everywhere.\n\nFor the region between consecutive points, I should use the minimum of the secants extending from the adjacent pairs, which ensures the upper bound stays tight. But I'm realizing the core issue: the direct secant between two points lies below the function (since it's log-concave), so the upper hull must rely on tangent lines at each evaluation point instead, where the tangent at x_j gives the upper bound in that region.\n\nFor computing the tangent slope without an explicit derivative, I can either use finite differences or bound it using the left and right secant slopes—the Gilks & Wild approach uses these secant slopes to constrain the tangent slope for a log-concave function.\n\nThe key property is that for a concave function, the true derivative at x_j lies between the left and right secant slopes, and I need to pick the right one to ensure the tangent line stays above the function everywhere. Let me work through the secant-based approach more carefully, since the secant from x_j to x_{j+1} actually lies below h between those points but above h outside that interval. So the upper hull between consecutive abscissae is the minimum of the line extending right from the previous pair and the line extending left from the next pair, with their intersection marking the breakpoint. For the boundary regions, I use the secant from the first two points on the left and the last two points on the right, though this requires at least four abscissae to work properly.\n\nActually, I {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_018aE8TPeCk3ENbC1wRPFfpV","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01WN6iGdhuqVosAqmhN3arFU","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/app/ars.R","content":"##############################################################################\n# Adaptive Rejection Sampling (ARS)\n# Based on Gilks, W. R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n##############################################################################\n\n# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n\n#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n#' @param x numeric vector of points\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\neval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n  vals <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n  log(vals)\n}\n\n#' Numerically compute the derivative of h(x) = log(f(x))\n#' Uses central differences with adaptive step size\n#' @param x points at which to evaluate derivative\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param eps step size for finite differences\n#' @return numeric vector of h'(x)\ncompute_h_deriv <- function(x, f, eps = 1e-7) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  deriv <- numeric(n)\n  for (i in 1:n) {\n    step <- max(abs(x[i]) * eps, eps)\n    h_plus <- eval_log_density(x[i] + step, f)\n    h_minus <- eval_log_density(x[i] - step, f)\n    deriv[i] <- (h_plus - h_minus) / (2 * step)\n  }\n  deriv\n}\n\n#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n#' Compute intersection points z of adjacent tangent lines\n#' Tangent at x_j: L_j(t) = hx[j] + hpx[j] * (t - x[j])\n#' z_{j+1} is the intersection of L_j and L_{j+1}\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density values\n#' @param hpx derivative of log-density at x\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @return vector of breakpoints (length n+1)\ncompute_z_points <- function(x, hx, hpx, lb, ub) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  z <- numeric(n + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[n + 1] <- ub\n  if (n >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(n - 1)) {\n      denom <- hpx[j] - hpx[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x[j] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - hpx[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + hpx[j] * x[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  # Ensure z is non-decreasing (numerical safety)\n  for (i in 2:length(z)) {\n    if (is.finite(z[i]) && is.finite(z[i - 1]) && z[i] < z[i - 1]) {\n      z[i] <- z[i - 1]\n    }\n  }\n  z\n}\n\n#' Evaluate the upper hull at arbitrary points\n#' @param t evaluation points\n#' @param x abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param hpx derivative at x\n#' @param z breakpoints\n#' @return upper hull values at t\neval_upper_hull <- function(t, x, hx, hpx, z) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  seg <- findInterval(t, z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n))\n  hx[seg] + hpx[seg] * (t - x[seg])\n}\n\n#' Evaluate the lower hull at arbitrary points\n#' @param t evaluation points\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return lower hull values at t\neval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n  if (any(inside)) {\n    ti <- t[inside]\n    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n  }\n  result\n}\n\n#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n#' Each piece j (from z[j] to z[j+1]) has:\n#'   u(t) = hx[j] + hpx[j]*(t - x[j]) = c_j + hpx[j]*t\n#' where c_j = hx[j] - hpx[j]*x[j]\n#' @param nsamp number of samples\n#' @param x abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param hpx derivative at x\n#' @param z breakpoints\n#' @return vector of samples\nsample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, x, hx, hpx, z) {\n  n <- length(x)\n\n  # Compute c_j for each piece\n  cj <- hx - hpx * x\n\n  # Integrate exp(c_j + hpx[j]*t) over [z[j], z[j+1]]\n  seg_integrals <- numeric(n)\n  for (j in 1:n) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- hpx[j]\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      if (sj <= 0) { seg_integrals[j] <- 0; next }\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj[j] + sj * b) / sj\n      next\n    }\n    if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      if (sj >= 0) { seg_integrals[j] <- 0; next }\n      seg_integrals[j] <- -exp(cj[j] + sj * a) / sj\n      next\n    }\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj[j]) * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj[j]) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n    }\n    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n    }\n  }\n\n  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n  }\n\n  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n  segments <- sample(1:n, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n\n  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n    j <- segments[i]\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- hpx[j]\n    u <- runif(1)\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      # sj > 0; CDF: F(t) = exp(sj*t)/exp(sj*b)\n      samples[i] <- b + log(u) / sj\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      # sj < 0; CDF: 1 - exp(sj*(t-a))\n      samples[i] <- a + log(1 - u) / sj\n    } else if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n    }\n    if (is.finite(a)) samples[i] <- max(a, samples[i])\n    if (is.finite(b)) samples[i] <- min(b, samples[i])\n  }\n  samples\n}\n\n#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\ninitialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n    vals <- f(test_pts)\n    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n    lb_eff <- center - 10\n    ub_eff <- center + 10\n  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n    ub_eff <- ub\n    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n  } else {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- ub\n  }\n\n  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n  x_init\n}\n\n#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n  }\n}\n\n# ---- Main ARS function ----\n\n#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n#'\n#' @param n number of samples to generate\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n\n  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n  }\n\n  # Initialize abscissae\n  x_abs <- initialize_abscissae(lb, ub, f, k)\n  x_abs <- sort(unique(x_abs))\n\n  # Evaluate log-density and its derivative at initial abscissae\n  hx <- eval_log_density(x_abs, f)\n  hpx <- compute_h_deriv(x_abs, f)\n\n  # Check initial log-concavity\n  check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n\n  # For bounded domains with infinite derivatives at boundaries, ensure\n  # first derivative is positive and last is negative (for log-concavity)\n  if (is.finite(lb) && hpx[1] < 0) {\n    # This means h is decreasing at the left boundary; for the upper hull\n    # to work with lb, we need the It's fine if the density is monotone decreasing.\n  }\n\n  # Main sampling loop\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  n_accepted <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (n_accepted < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Compute z breakpoints\n    z <- compute_z_points(x_abs, hx, hpx, lb, ub)\n\n    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, samples[n_accepted] <- x_star\n      }\n\n      # Update the abscissae (cap at 200)\n      if (length(x_abs) < 200) {\n        insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n        x_abs <- with new point\n        check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (n_accepted < n) {\n    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n R., & Wild, P. (1992)\n# \"Adaptive rejection sampling for Gibbs sampling\"\n##############################################################################\n\n# ---- Auxiliary / helper functions ----\n\n#' Evaluate the log-density, with safety checks\n#' @param x numeric vector of points\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized)\n#' @return numeric vector of log(f(x))\neval_log_density <- function(x, f) {\n  vals <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.na(vals) | is.nan(vals))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NA/NaN values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(vals < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  vals[vals == 0] <- .Machine$double.xmin\n  log(vals)\n}\n\n#' Numerically compute the derivative of h(x) = log(f(x))\n#' Uses central differences with adaptive step size\n#' @param x points at which to evaluate derivative\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param eps step size for finite differences\n#' @return numeric vector of h'(x)\ncompute_h_deriv <- function(x, f, eps = 1e-7) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  deriv <- numeric(n)\n  for (i in 1:n) {\n    step <- max(abs(x[i]) * eps, eps)\n    h_plus <- eval_log_density(x[i] + step, f)\n    h_minus <- eval_log_density(x[i] - step, f)\n    deriv[i] <- (h_plus - h_minus) / (2 * step)\n  }\n  deriv\n}\n\n#' Check log-concavity at a set of sorted abscissae\n#' @param x sorted numeric vector of abscissae (length >= 3)\n#' @param hx log-density evaluated at x\n#' @return TRUE if log-concave, otherwise stops with error\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  slopes <- diff(hx) / diff(x)\n  slope_diffs <- diff(slopes)\n  if (any(slope_diffs > 1e-6)) {\n    stop(\"Non-log-concave density detected: the log-density has increasing slopes.\")\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n#' Compute intersection points z of adjacent tangent lines\n#' Tangent at x_j: L_j(t) = hx[j] + hpx[j] * (t - x[j])\n#' z_{j+1} is the intersection of L_j and L_{j+1}\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density values\n#' @param hpx derivative of log-density at x\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @return vector of breakpoints (length n+1)\ncompute_z_points <- function(x, hx, hpx, lb, ub) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  z <- numeric(n + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[n + 1] <- ub\n  if (n >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(n - 1)) {\n      denom <- hpx[j] - hpx[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x[j] + x[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (hx[j + 1] - hx[j] - hpx[j + 1] * x[j + 1] + hpx[j] * x[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  # Ensure z is non-decreasing (numerical safety)\n  for (i in 2:length(z)) {\n    if (is.finite(z[i]) && is.finite(z[i - 1]) && z[i] < z[i - 1]) {\n      z[i] <- z[i - 1]\n    }\n  }\n  z\n}\n\n#' Evaluate the upper hull at arbitrary points\n#' @param t evaluation points\n#' @param x abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param hpx derivative at x\n#' @param z breakpoints\n#' @return upper hull values at t\neval_upper_hull <- function(t, x, hx, hpx, z) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  seg <- findInterval(t, z, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n))\n  hx[seg] + hpx[seg] * (t - x[seg])\n}\n\n#' Evaluate the lower hull at arbitrary points\n#' @param t evaluation points\n#' @param x sorted abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @return lower hull values at t\neval_lower_hull <- function(t, x, hx) {\n  n <- length(x)\n  result <- rep(-Inf, length(t))\n  inside <- t >= x[1] & t <= x[n]\n  if (any(inside)) {\n    ti <- t[inside]\n    seg <- findInterval(ti, x, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n    seg <- pmax(1, pmin(seg, n - 1))\n    frac <- (ti - x[seg]) / (x[seg + 1] - x[seg])\n    result[inside] <- hx[seg] + frac * (hx[seg + 1] - hx[seg])\n  }\n  result\n}\n\n#' Sample from the piecewise-exponential upper hull distribution\n#' Each piece j (from z[j] to z[j+1]) has:\n#'   u(t) = hx[j] + hpx[j]*(t - x[j]) = c_j + hpx[j]*t\n#' where c_j = hx[j] - hpx[j]*x[j]\n#' @param nsamp number of samples\n#' @param x abscissae\n#' @param hx log-density at x\n#' @param hpx derivative at x\n#' @param z breakpoints\n#' @return vector of samples\nsample_upper_hull <- function(nsamp, x, hx, hpx, z) {\n  n <- length(x)\n\n  # Compute c_j for each piece\n  cj <- hx - hpx * x\n\n  # Integrate exp(c_j + hpx[j]*t) over [z[j], z[j+1]]\n  seg_integrals <- numeric(n)\n  for (j in 1:n) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- hpx[j]\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      if (sj <= 0) { seg_integrals[j] <- 0; next }\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj[j] + sj * b) / sj\n      next\n    }\n    if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      if (sj >= 0) { seg_integrals[j] <- 0; next }\n      seg_integrals[j] <- -exp(cj[j] + sj * a) / sj\n      next\n    }\n    if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj[j]) * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- exp(cj[j]) * (exp(sj * b) - exp(sj * a)) / sj\n    }\n    if (is.na(seg_integrals[j]) || is.nan(seg_integrals[j]) || seg_integrals[j] < 0) {\n      seg_integrals[j] <- 0\n    }\n  }\n\n  total <- sum(seg_integrals)\n  if (total <= 0 || is.na(total) || is.infinite(total)) {\n    stop(\"Upper hull integral is non-positive or infinite. Check density and bounds.\")\n  }\n\n  probs <- seg_integrals / total\n  segments <- sample(1:n, size = nsamp, replace = TRUE, prob = probs)\n\n  samples <- numeric(nsamp)\n  for (i in 1:nsamp) {\n    j <- segments[i]\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    sj <- hpx[j]\n    u <- runif(1)\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      # sj > 0; CDF: F(t) = exp(sj*t)/exp(sj*b)\n      samples[i] <- b + log(u) / sj\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      # sj < 0; CDF: 1 - exp(sj*(t-a))\n      samples[i] <- a + log(1 - u) / sj\n    } else if (abs(sj) < 1e-10) {\n      samples[i] <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      ea <- exp(sj * a)\n      eb <- exp(sj * b)\n      val <- ea + u * (eb - ea)\n      if (val <= 0) val <- .Machine$double.xmin\n      samples[i] <- log(val) / sj\n    }\n    if (is.finite(a)) samples[i] <- max(a, samples[i])\n    if (is.finite(b)) samples[i] <- min(b, samples[i])\n  }\n  samples\n}\n\n#' Initialize starting abscissae for ARS\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param k number of initial points (default 5)\n#' @return sorted vector of initial abscissae\ninitialize_abscissae <- function(lb, ub, f, k = 5) {\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    test_pts <- seq(-5, 5, length.out = 21)\n    vals <- f(test_pts)\n    mode_idx <- which.max(vals)\n    center <- test_pts[mode_idx]\n    lb_eff <- center - 10\n    ub_eff <- center + 10\n  } else if (is.infinite(lb)) {\n    ub_eff <- ub\n    lb_eff <- ub - 20\n  } else if (is.infinite(ub)) {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- lb + 20\n  } else {\n    lb_eff <- lb\n    ub_eff <- ub\n  }\n\n  x_init <- seq(lb_eff, ub_eff, length.out = k + 2)\n  x_init <- x_init[2:(k + 1)]\n  x_init\n}\n\n#' Validate inputs to the ars function\n#' @param n number of samples\n#' @param f density function\n#' @param lb lower bound\n#' @param ub upper bound\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || is.na(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (n <= 0 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"Lower bound must be strictly less than upper bound.\")\n  }\n}\n\n# ---- Main ARS function ----\n\n#' Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n#'\n#' @param n number of samples to generate\n#' @param f density function (possibly unnormalized, vectorized)\n#' @param lb lower bound of the support (default -Inf)\n#' @param ub upper bound of the support (default Inf)\n#' @param k number of initial abscissae (default 5)\n#' @return numeric vector of n samples from the target distribution\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, k = 5) {\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub)\n\n  if (!is.numeric(k) || length(k) != 1 || k < 3) {\n    stop(\"'k' must be a numeric value >= 3.\")\n  }\n\n  # Initialize abscissae\n  x_abs <- positive and last is negative (for log-concavity)\n  if (is.finite(lb) && hpx[1] < 0) {\n    # This means h is decreasing at the left boundary; for the upper hull\n    # to work with lb, we need the first tangent to have positive slope\n    # OR lb is the left boundary. It's fine if the density is monotone decreasing.\n  }\n\n  # Main sampling loop\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  n_accepted <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (n_accepted < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Compute z breakpoints\n    z <- compute_z_points(x_abs, hx, hpx, lb, ub)\n\n    # Sample a candidate from the upper hull\n    x_star <- sample_upper_hull(1, x_abs, hx, hpx, z)\n\n    # Evaluate upper and lower hulls at x_star\n    u_star <- eval_upper_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx, hpx, z)\n    l_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, x_abs, hx)\n\n    # Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    if (w <= exp(l_star - u_star)) {\n      n_accepted <- n_accepted + 1\n      samples[n_accepted] <- x_star\n    } else {\n      # Evaluate the actual log-density\n      h_star <- eval_log_density(x_star, f)\n      hp_star <- compute_h_deriv(x_star, f)\n\n      # Rejection test\n      if (w <= exp(h_star - u_star)) {\n        n_accepted <- n_accepted + 1\n        samples[n_accepted] <- x_star\n      }\n\n      # Update the abscissae (cap at 200)\n      if (length(x_abs) < 200) {\n        insert_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n        x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n        hx <- append(hx, h_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n        hpx <- append(hpx, hp_star, after = insert_pos - 1)\n\n        # Re-check log-concavity with new point\n        check_log_concavity(x_abs, hx)\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (n_accepted < n) {\n    warning(\"ARS did not generate enough samples within the iteration limit.\")\n    return(samples[1:n_accepted])\n  }\n\n  samples\n}\n\n# ---- Test function ----\n\n#' Run formal tests of the ARS implementation\ntest <- function() {\n
